The StorageVersion manager\n// only needs to update one StorageVersion for the equivalent Groups.\nfunc dedupResourceInfos(infos []ResourceInfo) []ResourceInfo {\n\tvar ret []ResourceInfo\n\tseen := make(map[schema.GroupResource]struct{})\n\tfor _, info := range infos {\n\t\tgr := info.GroupResource\n\t\tif _, ok := seen[gr]; that manage API group storage version registration, specifically mapping v1beta1 to v1 equivalents.\\n\\n## REST Storage Providers with Version Registration\\n\\nThree REST storage providers define both v1beta1Storage() and v1Storage() methods, implementing the pattern of serving multiple API versions:\\n\\n1. **admissionregistration** (pkg/registry/admissionregistration/rest/storage_apiserver.go): Defines v1beta1Storage and v1Storage methods that register webhook configurations and validation/mutation policies across API versions.\\n\\n2. **authentication** (pkg/registry/authentication/rest/storage_authentication.go): Implements both v1Storage and v1beta1Storage methods for managing SelfSubjectAccessReviews and other authentication resources.\\n\\n3. **storage** (pkg/registry/storage/rest/storage_storage.go): Provides v1alpha1Storage, v1beta1Storage, and v1Storage methods for managing CSI drivers, nodes, storage capacity, classes, and volume attachments across multiple API versions.\\n\\n## StorageVersion Manager Interface\\n\\nThe core StorageVersion management system is defined in staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/storageversion/manager.go. The Manager interface provides:\\n- AddResourceInfo(): Records resources whose StorageVersions need updates\\n- UpdateStorageVersions(): Updates the StorageVersions in etcd\\n- PendingUpdate() and Completed(): Track update status\\n\\nThe ResourceInfo struct encapsulates the storage version metadata including:\\n- GroupResource: The API resource identifier\\n- EncodingVersion: The version used for etcd storage\\n- DirectlyDecodableVersions: Versions the converter knows how to decode\\n- ServedVersions: All versions served by the API server\\n- EquivalentResourceMapper: Maps equivalent resources across groups\\n\\n## ResourceEncodingConfig System\\n\\nThe ResourceEncodingConfig interface (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/storage/resource_encoding_config.go) controls which GroupVersion is used for etcd storage through:\\n- StorageEncodingFor(): Returns the serialization format for a resource\\n- InMemoryEncodingFor(): Returns the internal representation version\\n- SetResourceEncoding(): Overrides default encoding for specific resources\\n\\nThe DefaultResourceEncodingConfig implementation maintains a map of resource-specific overrides, allowing v1beta1 resources to be stored as v1 in etcd while maintaining backward compatibility.\\n\\n## Storage Version Registration Chain\\n\\nThe registration flow follows this chain:\\n\\n1. **API Server Initialization** (genericapiserver.go InstallAPIGroup): When installing an API group, the APIGroupVersion.InstallREST is called.\\n\\n2. **API Group Version Setup** (groupversion.go InstallREST): Creates an APIInstaller to register REST handlers and build ResourceInfo objects.\\n\\n3. **Resource Handler Registration** (installer.go Install and registerResourceHandlers): For each resource, creates ResourceInfo containing:\\n   - The EncodingVersion from StorageVersionProvider.StorageVersion()\\n   - Decodable versions from ConvertabilityChecker\\n   - Served versions from AllServedVersionsByResource\\n\\n4. **Storage Version Manager Registration**: The built ResourceInfo objects are passed to StorageVersionManager.AddResourceInfo(), which records them for updating the StorageVersion API objects.\\n\\n## Storage Factory Configuration\\n\\nThe default_storage_factory_builder.go NewStorageFactoryConfig() defines ResourceEncodingOverrides that explicitly set which version is stored in etcd:\\n- coordination.leasecandidates: v1alpha2 (not v1)\\n- networking.ipaddresses and servicecidrs: v1beta1 (not v1)\\n- admissionregistration policies: v1alpha1 (not v1)\\n- storage.volumeattributesclasses: v1beta1 (not v1)\\n\\nThese overrides are merged with the DefaultResourceEncodingConfig using MergeResourceEncodingConfigs() in helpers.go.\\n\\n## Storage Cohabitation\\n\\nThe storage_factory.go AddCohabitatingResources() method links resources that share the same underlying etcd storage, such as:\\n- apps.deployments and extensions.deployments\\n- networking.ingresses and extensions.ingresses\\n- api.events and events.k8s.io.events\\n\\nThis ensures that equivalent resources across API groups use the same storage location and version encoding.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
